[30;1m339 | [0m[35m:class:`~django_otp.plugins.otp_totp.models.TOTPDevice` matches a token in the[0m
[30;1m340 | [0m[35mpast or future, it will update[0m
[30;1m341 | [0m[35m:attr:`~django_otp.plugins.otp_totp.models.TOTPDevice.drift` to the number of[0m
[30;1m342 | [0m[35mtime steps that the two sides are out of sync. For subsequent tokens, we'll[0m
[30;1m343 | [0m[35mslide the window of acceptable tokens by this number.[0m
[30;1m344 | [0m[35m[0m

[30;1m170 | [0m[35mare subclassed from :class:`django_otp.models.Device`. Each model class supports[0m
[30;1m171 | [0m[35ma single type of OTP device. Remember that when we use the term :term:`device`[0m

[30;1m67 | [0m[35m        *BooleanField*: A boolean value that tells us whether this device has[0m
